repository root for full details.\n*/\n\nimport { M_BEACON, type Room, Thread, type MatrixEvent, EventType, type MatrixClient } from \"matrix-js-sdk/src/matrix\";\nimport { logger } from \"matrix-js-sdk/src/logger\";\n\nimport shouldHideEvent from \"./shouldHideEvent\";\nimport { haveRendererForEvent } from \"./events/EventTileFactory\";\nimport { RoomNotifState, getRoomNotifsState } from \"./RoomNotifs\";\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this event arriving in a room should affect the room's\n * count of unread messages\n *\n * @param client The Matrix Client instance of the logged-in user\n * @param {Object} ev The event\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given event should affect the unread message count\n */\nexport function eventTriggersUnreadCount(client: MatrixClient, ev: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    if (ev.getSender() === client.getSafeUserId()) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    switch (ev.getType()) {\n        case EventType.RoomMember:\n        case EventType.RoomThirdPartyInvite:\n        case EventType.CallAnswer:\n        case EventType.CallHangup:\n        case EventType.RoomCanonicalAlias:\n        case EventType.RoomServerAcl:\n        case M_BEACON.name:\n        case M_BEACON.altName:\n            return false;\n    }\n\n    if (ev.isRedacted()) return false;\n    try {\n        return haveRendererForEvent(ev, client, false /* hidden messages should never trigger unread counts anyways */);\n    } catch (e) {\n        console.warn(\"Error determining if event should trigger unread count\", e);\n        return false; // If we can't determine if the event should trigger an unread count, assume it does not.\n    }\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room, includeThreads: boolean): boolean {\n    const toCheck: Array<Room | Thread> = [room];\n    if (includeThreads) {\n        toCheck.push(...room.getThreads());\n    }\n\n    for (const withTimeline of toCheck) {\n        if (doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(room, withTimeline.timeline)) {\n            // We found an unread, so the room is unread\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we got here then no timelines were found with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): boolean {\n    // The room is a space, let's ignore it\n    if (room.isSpaceRoom()) return false;\n\n    const myUserId = room.client.getSafeUserId();\n    const latestImportantEventId = findLatestImportantEvent(room.client, timeline)?.getId();\n    if (latestImportantEventId) {\n        return !room.hasUserReadEvent(myUserId, latestImportantEventId);\n    } else {\n        // We couldn't find an important event to check - check the unimportant ones.\n        const earliestUnimportantEventId = timeline.at(0)?.getId();\n        if (!earliestUnimportantEventId) {\n            // There are no events in this timeline - it is uninitialised, so we\n            // consider it read\n            return false;\n        } else if (room.hasUserReadEvent(myUserId, earliestUnimportantEventId)) {\n            // Some of the unimportant events are read, and there are no\n            // important ones after them, so we've read everything.\n            return false;\n        } else {\n            // We have events. and none of them are read.  We must guess that\n            // the timeline is unread, because there could be older unread\n            // important events that we don't have loaded.\n            logger.warn(\"Falling back to unread room because of no read receipt or counting message found\", {\n                roomId: room.roomId,\n                earliestUnimportantEventId: earliestUnimportantEventId,\n            });\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this room has unread threads.\n * @param room The room to check\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given room has unread threads\n */\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadThreads(room: Room): boolean {\n    if (getRoomNotifsState(room.client, room.roomId) === RoomNotifState.Mute) {\n        // No unread for muted rooms, nor their threads\n        // NB. This logic duplicated in RoomNotifs.determineUnreadState\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n        if (doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(room, thread.timeline)) {\n            // We found an unread, so the room has an unread thread\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we got here then no threads were found with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread): boolean {\n    const room = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.room : roomOrThread;\n    const events = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.timeline : room.getLiveTimeline().getEvents();\n    return doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(room, events);\n}\n\n/**\n * Look backwards through the timeline and find the last event that is\n * \"important\" in the sense of isImportantEvent.\n *\n * @returns the latest important event, or null if none were found\n */\nfunction findLatestImportantEvent(client: MatrixClient, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): MatrixEvent | null {\n    for (let index = timeline.length - 1; index >= 0; index--) {\n        const event = timeline[index];\n        if (isImportantEvent(client, event)) {\n            return event;\n        }\n    }\n    return null;\n}\n\n/**\n * Given this event does not have a receipt, is it important enough to make\n * this room unread?\n */\nfunction isImportantEvent(client: MatrixClient, event: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    return !shouldHideEvent(event) && eventTriggersUnreadCount(client, event);\n}\n","numLines":151,"startLine":1,"totalLines":151}}}
{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_0188yrZv12meZZgbf7Vx3QJ4","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I understand the current implementation. The problem is that the `doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages` function is being called with threads, but it's using `room.hasUserReadEvent()` which only checks main timeline receipts, not thread-scoped receipts.\n\nLooking at the test cases again:\n\n1. Line 267-305: \"returns false for a room with read thread messages\"\n   - Creates a thread and adds a thread-scoped receipt\n   - Expects the thread to be read\n   - But `room.hasUserReadEvent()` won't find the thread-scoped receipt\n\n2. Line 307-345: \"returns true for a room when read receipt is not on the latest thread messages\"\n   - Creates a thread and adds a thread-scoped receipt to the first event (not the latest)\n   - Expects the thread to be unread\n   - This also relies on properly finding thread-scoped receipts\n\nThe fix needs to:\n1. When checking a thread timeline, look for thread-scoped receipts (with thread_id in the receipt)\n2. Pass the thread ID to the checking function so it can look for the right receipt type\n\nHowever, there's a problem: the `doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages` function doesn't currently know if it's checking a thread or the room timeline. It receives a `room` and a `timeline`, but doesn't know the thread ID.\n\nLooking at the callers:\n- `doesRoomHaveUnreadMessages` passes `room.getLiveTimeline().getEvents()` for the room and `thread.timeline` for threads\n- `doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages` passes `roomOrThread.timeline` for both room and threads\n- `doesRoomHaveUnreadThreads` passes `thread.timeline` for threads\n\nSo I need to:\n1. doesRoomHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room, includeThreads: boolean): boolean {\n    const toCheck: Array<Room | Thread> = [room];\n    if (includeThreads) {\n        toCheck.push(...room.getThreads());\n \"./shouldHideEvent\";\nimport { haveRendererForEvent } from \"./events/EventTileFactory\";\nimport { RoomNotifState, getRoomNotifsState } from \"./RoomNotifs\";\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this event arriving in a room should affect the room's\n * count of unread messages\n *\n * @param client The Matrix Client instance of the logged-in user\n * @param {Object} ev The event\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given event should affect the unread message count\n */\nexport function eventTriggersUnreadCount(client: MatrixClient, ev: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    if (ev.getSender() === client.getSafeUserId()) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    switch (ev.getType()) {\n        case EventType.RoomMember:\n        case EventType.RoomThirdPartyInvite:\n        case EventType.CallAnswer:\n        case EventType.CallHangup:\n        case EventType.RoomCanonicalAlias:\n        case EventType.RoomServerAcl:\n        case M_BEACON.name:\n        case M_BEACON.altName:\n            return false;\n    }\n\n    if (ev.isRedacted()) return false;\n    try {\n        return haveRendererForEvent(ev, client, false /* hidden messages should never trigger unread counts anyways */);\n    } catch (e) {\n        console.warn(\"Error determining if event should trigger unread count\", e);\n        return false; // If we can't determine if the event should trigger an unread count, assume it does not.\n    }\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room, includeThreads: boolean): boolean {\n    const toCheck: Array<Room | Thread> = [room];\n    if (includeThreads) {\n        toCheck.push(...room.getThreads());\n    }\n\n    for (const withTimeline of toCheck) {\n        if (doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(room, withTimeline.timeline)) {\n            // We found an unread, so the room is unread\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we got here then no timelines were found with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): boolean {\n    // The room is a space, let's ignore it\n    if (room.isSpaceRoom()) return false;\n\n    const myUserId = room.client.getSafeUserId();\n    const latestImportantEventId = findLatestImportantEvent(room.client, timeline)?.getId();\n    if (latestImportantEventId) {\n        return !room.hasUserReadEvent(myUserId, latestImportantEventId);\n    } else {\n        // We couldn't find an important event to check - check the unimportant ones.\n        const earliestUnimportantEventId = timeline.at(0)?.getId();\n        if (!earliestUnimportantEventId) {\n            // There are no events in this timeline - it is uninitialised, so we\n            // consider it read\n            return false;\n        } else if (room.hasUserReadEvent(myUserId, earliestUnimportantEventId)) {\n            // Some of the unimportant events are read, and there are no\n            // important ones after them, so we've read everything.\n            return false;\n        } else {\n            // We have events. and none of them are read. repository root for full details.\n*/\n\nimport { M_BEACON, type Room, Thread, type MatrixEvent, EventType, type MatrixClient } from \"matrix-js-sdk/src/matrix\";\nimport { logger } from \"matrix-js-sdk/src/logger\";\n\nimport shouldHideEvent from \"./shouldHideEvent\";\nimport { haveRendererForEvent } from \"./events/EventTileFactory\";\nimport { RoomNotifState, getRoomNotifsState } from \"./RoomNotifs\";\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this event arriving in a room should affect the room's\n * count of unread messages\n *\n * @param client The Matrix Client instance of the logged-in user\n * @param {Object} ev The event\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given event should affect the unread message count\n */\nexport function eventTriggersUnreadCount(client: MatrixClient, ev: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    if (ev.getSender() === client.getSafeUserId()) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    switch (ev.getType()) {\n        case EventType.RoomMember:\n        case EventType.RoomThirdPartyInvite:\n        case EventType.CallAnswer:\n        case EventType.CallHangup:\n        case EventType.RoomCanonicalAlias:\n        case EventType.RoomServerAcl:\n        case M_BEACON.name:\n        case M_BEACON.altName:\n            return false;\n    }\n\n    if (ev.isRedacted()) return false;\n    try {\n        return haveRendererForEvent(ev, client, false /* hidden messages should never trigger unread counts anyways */);\n    } catch (e) {\n        console.warn(\"Error determining if event should trigger unread count\", e);\n        return false; // If we can't determine if the event should trigger an unread count, assume it does not.\n    }\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room, includeThreads: boolean): boolean {\n    // Check main timeline\n    if (doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(room)) {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    // Check threads if requested\n    if (includeThreads) {\n        for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n            if (doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(thread)) {\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we got here then no timelines were found with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>, threadId?: string): boolean {\n    const room = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.room : roomOrThread;\n\n    // The room is a space, let's ignore it\n    if (room.isSpaceRoom()) return false;\n\n    const myUserId = room.client.getSafeUserId();\n    const latestImportantEventId = findLatestImportantEvent(room.client, timeline)?.getId();\n    if (latestImportantEventId) {\n        return !hasUserReadEvent(roomOrThread, myUserId, latestImportantEventId);\n    } else {\n        // We couldn't find an important event to check - check the unimportant ones.\n        const earliestUnimportantEventId = timeline.at(0)?.getId();\n        if (!earliestUnimportantEventId) {\n            // There are no events in this timeline - it is uninitialised, so we\n            // consider it read\n            return false;\n        } else if (hasUserReadEvent(roomOrThread, myUserId, earliestUnimportantEventId)) {\n            // Some of the unimportant events are read, and there are no\n            // important ones after them, so we've read everything.\n            return false;\n        } else {\n            // We have events. and none of them are read.  We must guess that\n            // the timeline is unread, because there could be older unread\n            // important events that we don't have loaded.\n            logger.warn(\"Falling back to unread room because of no read receipt or counting message found\", {\n                roomId: room.roomId,\n                earliestUnimportantEventId: earliestUnimportantEventId,\n            });\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a user has read an event, considering thread-scoped receipts when applicable.\n *\n * @param roomOrThread The room or thread to check receipts in\n * @param userId The user ID to check for\n * @param eventId The event ID to check\n * @returns true if the user has read this event\n */\nfunction hasUserReadEvent(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, userId: string, eventId: string): boolean {\n    if (roomOrThread instanceof Thread) {\n        // For threads, we need to check thread-scoped receipts\n        return roomOrThread.hasUserReadEvent(userId, eventId);\n    } else {\n        // For rooms, check both threaded and unthreaded receipts\n        return roomOrThread.hasUserReadEvent(userId, eventId);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this room has unread threads.\n * @param room The room to check\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given room has unread threads\n */\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadThreads(room: Room): boolean {\n    if (getRoomNotifsState(room.client, room.roomId) === RoomNotifState.Mute) {\n        // No unread for muted rooms, nor their threads\n        // NB. This logic duplicated in RoomNotifs.determineUnreadState\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n        if (doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(thread, thread.timeline, thread.id)) {\n            // We found an unread, so the room has an unread thread\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we got here then no threads were found with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread): boolean {\n    const events = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.timeline : roomOrThread.getLiveTimeline().getEvents();\n    const threadId = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.id : undefined;\n    return doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread, events, threadId);\n}\n\n/**\n * Look backwards through the timeline and find the last event that is\n * \"important\" in the sense of isImportantEvent.\n *\n * @returns the latest important event, or null if none were found\n */\nfunction findLatestImportantEvent(client: MatrixClient, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): MatrixEvent | null {\n    for (let index = timeline.length - 1; index >= 0; index--) {\n        const event = timeline[index];\n        if (isImportantEvent(client, event)) {\n            return event;\n        }\n    }\n    return null;\n}\n\n/**\n * Given this event does not have a receipt, is it important enough to make\n * this room unread?\n */\nfunction isImportantEvent(client: MatrixClient, event: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    return !shouldHideEvent(event) && eventTriggersUnreadCount(client, event);\n}\n","numLines":173,"startLine":1,"totalLines":173}}}

\"./events/EventTileFactory\";\nimport { RoomNotifState, getRoomNotifsState } from \"./RoomNotifs\";\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this event arriving in a room should affect the room's\n * count of unread messages\n *\n * @param client The Matrix Client instance of the logged-in user\n * @param {Object} ev The event\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given event should affect the unread message count\n */\nexport function eventTriggersUnreadCount(client: MatrixClient, ev: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    if (ev.getSender() === client.getSafeUserId()) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    switch (ev.getType()) {\n        case EventType.RoomMember:\n        case EventType.RoomThirdPartyInvite:\n        case EventType.CallAnswer:\n        case EventType.CallHangup:\n        case EventType.RoomCanonicalAlias:\n        case EventType.RoomServerAcl:\n        case M_BEACON.name:\n        case M_BEACON.altName:\n            return false;\n    }\n\n    if (ev.isRedacted()) return if event should trigger unread count\", e);\n        return false; // If we can't determine if the event should trigger an unread count, assume it does not.\n    }\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room, includeThreads: boolean): boolean {\n    // Check main timeline\n    if (doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(room)) {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    // Check threads if requested\n    if (includeThreads) {\n        for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n            if (doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(thread)) {\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we got here then no timelines were found with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>, threadId?: string): boolean {\n    const room = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.room : roomOrThread;\n\n    // The room is a space, let's ignore it\n    if (room.isSpaceRoom()) return false;\n\n    const myUserId = room.client.getSafeUserId();\n    const latestImportantEventId = findLatestImportantEvent(room.client, timeline)?.getId();\n    if (latestImportantEventId) {\n        return !hasUserReadEvent(roomOrThread, myUserId, latestImportantEventId);\n    } else {\n        // We couldn't find an important event to check - check the unimportant ones.\n        const earliestUnimportantEventId = timeline.at(0)?.getId();\n        if (!earliestUnimportantEventId) {\n            // There are no events in this timeline - it is uninitialised, so we\n            // consider it read\n            return false;\n        } else if (hasUserReadEvent(roomOrThread, myUserId, earliestUnimportantEventId)) {\n            // Some of the unimportant events are read, and there are no\n            // important ones after them, so we've read everything.\n            return false;\n        } else {\n            // We have events. and none of them are read.  We must guess that\n            // the timeline is unread, because there could be older unread\n            // important events that we don't have loaded.\n            logger.warn(\"Falling back to unread room because of no read receipt or counting message found\", {\n                roomId: room.roomId,\n                earliestUnimportantEventId: earliestUnimportantEventId,\n            });\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a user has read an event, considering thread-scoped receipts when applicable.\n *\n * @param roomOrThread The room or thread to check receipts in\n * @param userId The user ID to check for\n * @param eventId The event ID to check\n * @returns true if the user has read this event\n */\nfunction hasUserReadEvent(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, userId: string, eventId: string): boolean {\n    if (roomOrThread instanceof Thread) {\n        // For threads, we need to check thread-scoped receipts\n        return roomOrThread.hasUserReadEvent(userId, eventId);\n    } else {\n        // For rooms, check both threaded and unthreaded receipts\n        return roomOrThread.hasUserReadEvent(userId, eventId);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this room has unread threads.\n * @param room The room to check\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given room has unread threads\n */\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadThreads(room: Room): boolean {\n    if (getRoomNotifsState(room.client, room.roomId) === RoomNotifState.Mute) {\n        // No unread for muted rooms, nor their threads\n        // NB. This logic duplicated in RoomNotifs.determineUnreadState\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n        if (doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(thread, thread.timeline, thread.id)) {\n            // We found an unread, so the room has an unread thread\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we got here then no threads were found with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread): boolean {\n    const events = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.timeline : roomOrThread.getLiveTimeline().getEvents();\n    const threadId = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.id : undefined;\n    return doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread, events, threadId);\n}\n\n/**\n * Look backwards through the timeline and find the last event that is\n * \"important\" in the sense of isImportantEvent.\n *\n * @returns the latest important event, or null if none were found\n */\nfunction findLatestImportantEvent(client: MatrixClient, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): MatrixEvent | null {\n    for (let index = timeline.length - 1; index >= 0; index--) {\n        const event = timeline[index];\n        if (isImportantEvent(client, event)) {\n            return event;\n        }\n    }\n    return null;\n}\n\n/**\n * Given this event does not have a receipt, is it important enough to make\n * this room unread?\n */\nfunction isImportantEvent(client: MatrixClient, event: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    return !shouldHideEvent(event) && eventTriggersUnreadCount(client, event);\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":66,"oldLines":7,"newStart":66,"newLines":7,"lines":["     return false;"," }"," ","-function doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>, threadId?: string): boolean {","+function doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): boolean {","     const room = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? arriving in a room should affect the room's\n * count of unread messages\n *\n * @param client The Matrix Client instance of the logged-in user\n * @param {Object} ev The event\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given event should affect the unread message count\n */\nexport function eventTriggersUnreadCount(client: MatrixClient, ev: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    if (ev.getSender() === client.getSafeUserId()) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    switch (ev.getType()) {\n        case EventType.RoomMember:\n        case EventType.RoomThirdPartyInvite:\n        case EventType.CallAnswer:\n        case EventType.CallHangup:\n        case EventType.RoomCanonicalAlias:\n        case EventType.RoomServerAcl:\n        case M_BEACON.name:\n        case M_BEACON.altName:\n            return false;\n    }\n\n    if (ev.isRedacted()) return false;\n    try {\n        return haveRendererForEvent(ev, client, false /* hidden messages should never trigger unread counts anyways */);\n    } catch (e) {\n        console.warn(\"Error determining if event should trigger unread count\", e);\n        return false; // If we can't determine if the event should trigger an unread count, assume it does not.\n    }\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadMessages(room: Room, includeThreads: boolean): boolean {\n    // Check main timeline\n    if (doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(room)) {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    // Check threads if requested\n    if (includeThreads) {\n        for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n return false;\n}\n\nfunction doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): boolean {\n    const room = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.room : roomOrThread;\n\n    // The room is a space, let's ignore it\n    if (room.isSpaceRoom()) return false;\n\n    const myUserId = room.client.getSafeUserId();\n    const latestImportantEventId = // We couldn't find an important event to check - check the unimportant ones.\n        const earliestUnimportantEventId = timeline.at(0)?.getId();\n        if (!earliestUnimportantEventId) {\n earliestUnimportantEventId)) {\n            // Some of the unimportant events are read, and there are no\n            // important ones after them, so we've read everything.\n            return false;\n        } else {\n            // We have events. and none of them are read.  We must guess that\n            // the timeline is unread, because there could be older unread\n            // important events that we don't have loaded.\n            logger.warn(\"Falling back to unread room because of no read receipt or counting message found\", {\n                roomId: room.roomId,\n                earliestUnimportantEventId: earliestUnimportantEventId,\n            });\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a user has read an event, considering thread-scoped receipts when applicable.\n *\n * @param roomOrThread The room or thread to check receipts in\n * @param userId The user ID to check for\n * @param eventId The event ID to check\n * @returns true if the user has read this event\n */\nfunction hasUserReadEvent(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, userId: string, eventId: string): boolean {\n    if (roomOrThread instanceof Thread) {\n        // For threads, we need to check thread-scoped receipts\n        return roomOrThread.hasUserReadEvent(userId, eventId);\n    } else {\n        // For rooms, check both threaded and unthreaded receipts\n        return roomOrThread.hasUserReadEvent(userId, eventId);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this room has unread threads.\n * @param room The room to check\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given room has unread threads\n */\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadThreads(room: Room): boolean {\n    if (getRoomNotifsState(room.client, room.roomId) === RoomNotifState.Mute) {\n        // No unread for muted rooms, nor their threads\n        // NB. This logic duplicated in RoomNotifs.determineUnreadState\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n        if (doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(thread, thread.timeline, thread.id)) {\n            // We found an unread, so the room has an unread thread\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we got here then no threads were found with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread): boolean {\n    const events = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.timeline : roomOrThread.getLiveTimeline().getEvents();\n    const threadId = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.id : undefined;\n    return doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread, events, threadId);\n}\n\n/**\n * Look backwards through the timeline and find the last event that is\n * \"important\" in the sense of isImportantEvent.\n *\n * @returns the latest important event, or null if none were found\n */\nfunction findLatestImportantEvent(client: MatrixClient, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): MatrixEvent | null {\n    for (let index = timeline.length - 1; index >= 0; index--) {\n        const event = timeline[index];\n        if (isImportantEvent(client, event)) {\n            return event;\n        }\n    }\n    return null;\n}\n\n/**\n * Given this event does not have a receipt, is it important enough to make\n * this room unread?\n */\nfunction isImportantEvent(client: MatrixClient, event: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    return !shouldHideEvent(event) && eventTriggersUnreadCount(client, event);\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":131,"oldLines":7,"newStart":131,"newLines":7,"lines":["     }"," ","     for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {","-        if (doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(thread, thread.timeline, thread.id)) {","+        if (doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(thread, thread.timeline)) {","             // We found an unread, so the room has an unread thread","             return true;","         }"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

When all events in a timeline are from the current user, the latest important event will be null (since the current user's events don't trigger unread). But then the code falls back to checking receipts on unimportant events, which can incorrectly return true. \n\nLet me fix this by checking if the latest event was sent by the current user:"}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":154,"cache_read_input_tokens":89506,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":154},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3dc39fc0-c5a7-4f66-a259-93c5c10ec7be","uuid":"cc5f6f16-9738-4fdb-8a50-08d5e03ef22f"}

timeline\n    if (doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(room)) {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    // Check threads if requested\n    if (includeThreads) {\n        for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n            if (doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(thread)) {\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we got here then no timelines were found with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): boolean {\n    const room = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.room : roomOrThread;\n\n    // The room is a space, let's ignore it\n    if (room.isSpaceRoom()) return false;\n\n    const myUserId = room.client.getSafeUserId();\n    const latestImportantEventId = findLatestImportantEvent(room.client, timeline)?.getId();\n    if (latestImportantEventId) {\n        return !hasUserReadEvent(roomOrThread, myUserId, latestImportantEventId);\n    } else {\n        // We couldn't find an important event to check.\n        // If the latest event was sent by the current user, it won't trigger unread,\n        // so the timeline is read.\n        const latestEvent = timeline.at(-1);\n        if (latestEvent?.getSender() === myUserId) {\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        // Check the unimportant events\n        const earliestUnimportantEventId = timeline.at(0)?.getId();\n        if (!earliestUnimportantEventId) {\n            // There are no events in this timeline - it is uninitialised, so we\n            // consider it read\n            return false;\n        } else if (hasUserReadEvent(roomOrThread, myUserId, earliestUnimportantEventId)) {\n            // Some of the unimportant events are read, and there are no\n            // important ones after them, so we've read everything.\n            return false;\n        } else {\n            // We have events. and none of them are read.  We must guess that\n            // the timeline is unread, because there could be older unread\n            // important events that we don't have loaded.\n            logger.warn(\"Falling back to unread room because of no read receipt or counting message found\", {\n                roomId: room.roomId,\n                earliestUnimportantEventId: earliestUnimportantEventId,\n            });\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a user has read an event, considering thread-scoped receipts when applicable.\n *\n * @param roomOrThread The room or thread to check receipts in\n * @param userId The user ID to check for\n * @param eventId The event ID to check\n * @returns true if the user has read this event\n */\nfunction hasUserReadEvent(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, userId: string, eventId: string): boolean {\n    if (roomOrThread instanceof Thread) {\n        // For threads, we need to check thread-scoped receipts\n        return roomOrThread.hasUserReadEvent(userId, eventId);\n    } else {\n        // For rooms, check both threaded and unthreaded receipts\n        return roomOrThread.hasUserReadEvent(userId, eventId);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Returns true if this room has unread threads.\n * @param room The room to check\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given room has unread threads\n */\nexport function doesRoomHaveUnreadThreads(room: Room): boolean {\n    if (getRoomNotifsState(room.client, room.roomId) === RoomNotifState.Mute) {\n        // No unread for muted rooms, nor their threads\n        // NB. This logic duplicated in RoomNotifs.determineUnreadState\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    for (const thread of room.getThreads()) {\n        if (doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(thread, thread.timeline)) {\n            // We found an unread, so the room has an unread thread\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we got here then no threads were found with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nexport function doesRoomOrThreadHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread): boolean {\n    const events = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.timeline : roomOrThread.getLiveTimeline().getEvents();\n    return doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread, events);\n}\n\n/**\n * Look backwards through the timeline and find the last event that is\n * \"important\" in the sense of isImportantEvent.\n *\n * @returns the latest important event, or null if none were found\n */\nfunction findLatestImportantEvent(client: MatrixClient, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): MatrixEvent | null {\n    for (let index = timeline.length - 1; index >= 0; index--) {\n        const event = timeline[index];\n        if (isImportantEvent(client, event)) {\n            return event;\n        }\n    }\n    return null;\n}\n\n/**\n * Given this event does not have a receipt, is it important enough to make\n * this room unread?\n */\nfunction isImportantEvent(client: MatrixClient, event: MatrixEvent): boolean {\n    return !shouldHideEvent(event) && eventTriggersUnreadCount(client, event);\n}\n","numLines":180,"startLine":1,"totalLines":180}}}

user\n * @param {Object} ev The event\n * @returns {boolean} True if the given event should affect the unread message count\n */\nexport function eventTriggersUnreadCount(client: MatrixClient, ev: with unread messages.\n    return false;\n}\n\nfunction doesTimelineHaveUnreadMessages(roomOrThread: Room | Thread, timeline: Array<MatrixEvent>): boolean {\n    const room = roomOrThread instanceof Thread ? roomOrThread.room : roomOrThread;\n\n    // The room is a space, let's ignore it\n    if (room.isSpaceRoom()) return false;\n\n    const myUserId = room.client.getSafeUserId();\n    const
